<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" width="30" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="1376" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1917" class="extiw" title="commons:Category:1917">1917</a></b></i>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>1917 (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MCMXVII</a>)</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Common_year" title="Common year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Monday" title="Common year starting on Monday">starting on Monday</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>&#160;and a <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Sunday" title="Common year starting on Sunday">common year starting on Sunday</a> (<a href="/wiki/Dominical_letter" title="Dominical letter">dominical letter</a> A) of the <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">Julian calendar</a>, the 1917th year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 917th year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd&#160;millennium</a>, the 17th year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th&#160;century</a>, and the 8th year of the <a href="/wiki/1910s" title="1910s">1910s</a> decade. As of the start of 1917, the Gregorian calendar was 13 days ahead of the Julian calendar, which remained in localized use until 1923.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Below, events of <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> have the "WWI" prefix.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/January_1917" title="January 1917">January 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_1" title="January 1">January 1</a> – The <a href="/wiki/University_of_Oregon" title="University of Oregon">University of Oregon</a> defeats the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Pennsylvania" title="University of Pennsylvania">University of Pennsylvania</a> 14–0 in U.S. <a href="/wiki/College_football" title="College football">college football</a>'s 3rd Annual <a href="/wiki/Rose_Bowl_Game" title="Rose Bowl Game">Rose Bowl Game</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_2" title="January 2">January 2</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Royal_Bank_of_Canada" title="Royal Bank of Canada">Royal Bank of Canada</a> takes over <a href="/wiki/Quebec_Bank" title="Quebec Bank">Quebec Bank</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_3" title="January 3">January 3</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Ratho_rail_crash" title="Ratho rail crash">Ratho rail crash</a> in which <a href="/wiki/NBR_H_class" title="NBR H class">NBR H class</a> locomotive 874 <i>Dunedin</i> in charge of the Edinburgh to Glasgow express train was in collision with a <a href="/wiki/Light_engine" class="mw-redirect" title="Light engine">light engine</a> at Queensferry Junction, leaving 12 people dead and 46 seriously injured. The cause was found to be inadequate signalling procedures.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_9" title="January 9">January 9</a> – WWI: The last substantial <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Ottoman Army">Ottoman Army</a> garrison on the <a href="/wiki/Sinai_Peninsula" title="Sinai Peninsula">Sinai Peninsula</a> is captured by the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Desert_Column" title="Desert Column">Desert Column</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Rafa" title="Battle of Rafa">Battle of Rafa</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_11" title="January 11">January 11</a> – Unknown saboteurs set off the <a href="/wiki/Kingsland_Explosion" class="mw-redirect" title="Kingsland Explosion">Kingsland Explosion</a> at Kingsland (modern-day <a href="/wiki/Lyndhurst,_New_Jersey" title="Lyndhurst, New Jersey">Lyndhurst, New Jersey</a>), one of the events leading to United States involvement in WWI.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_16" title="January 16">January 16</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Virgin_Islands" title="Virgin Islands">Danish West Indies</a> is sold to the United States for $25 million.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_19" title="January 19">January 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Silvertown_explosion" title="Silvertown explosion">Silvertown explosion</a>: A blast at a munitions factory in London kills 73 and injures over 400. The resulting fire causes over £2,000,000 worth of damage.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_22" title="January 22">January 22</a> – WWI: President of the United States <a href="/wiki/Woodrow_Wilson" title="Woodrow Wilson">Woodrow Wilson</a> calls for "peace without victory" in Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_25" title="January 25">January 25</a>
<ul>
<li>WWI: British <a href="/wiki/Armed_merchantman" title="Armed merchantman">armed merchantman</a> <a href="/wiki/SS_Laurentic_(1908)" title="SS Laurentic (1908)">SS&#160;<i>Laurentic</i></a> is sunk by mines off <a href="/wiki/Lough_Swilly" title="Lough Swilly">Lough Swilly</a> (Ireland) with the loss of 354 of the 475 aboard.</li>
<li>An anti-<a href="/wiki/Prostitution" title="Prostitution">prostitution</a> drive in <a href="/wiki/Prostitution_in_the_United_States#Other_developments" title="Prostitution in the United States">San Francisco</a> occurs and police close about 200 prostitution houses.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_26" title="January 26">January 26</a> – The sea defences at the English village of <a href="/wiki/Hallsands" title="Hallsands">Hallsands</a> are breached, leading to all but one of the houses becoming uninhabitable.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_28" title="January 28">January 28</a> – The United States ends its search for <a href="/wiki/Pancho_Villa" title="Pancho Villa">Pancho Villa</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_30" title="January 30">January 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/John_J._Pershing" title="John J. Pershing">Pershing</a>'s troops in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> begin withdrawing back to the United States. They reach <a href="/wiki/Columbus,_New_Mexico" title="Columbus, New Mexico">Columbus, New Mexico</a> <a href="/wiki/February_5" title="February 5">February 5</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/February_1917" title="February 1917">February 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_1" title="February 1">February 1</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_U-boat_campaign_of_World_War_I" title="Atlantic U-boat campaign of World War I">Atlantic U-boat Campaign</a>: Germany announces its <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boats</a> will resume <a href="/wiki/Unrestricted_submarine_warfare" title="Unrestricted submarine warfare">unrestricted submarine warfare</a>, rescinding the '<a href="/wiki/Sussex_pledge" title="Sussex pledge"><i>Sussex</i> pledge</a>'.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_3" title="February 3">February 3</a> – WWI: The United States severs diplomatic relations with <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">Germany</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_5" title="February 5">February 5</a> – The new constitution of Mexico is adopted.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_13" title="February 13">February 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mata_Hari" title="Mata Hari">Mata Hari</a> is arrested in Paris for spying.</li>
<li>WWI: Beginning of the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Nekhl" title="Raid on Nekhl">Raid on Nekhl</a> by units of the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a>, to complete reoccupation of the <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egyptian</a> Sinai Peninsula.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_21" title="February 21">February 21</a> – British <a href="/wiki/Troopship" title="Troopship">troopship</a> <a href="/wiki/SS_Mendi" title="SS Mendi">SS&#160;<i>Mendi</i></a> is accidentally rammed and sunk off the <a href="/wiki/Isle_of_Wight" title="Isle of Wight">Isle of Wight</a>, killing 646, mainly members of the <a href="/wiki/South_African_Native_Labour_Corps" title="South African Native Labour Corps">South African Native Labour Corps</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Mendi_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mendi-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_24" title="February 24">February 24</a> – WWI: United States ambassador to the United Kingdom, <a href="/wiki/Walter_Hines_Page" title="Walter Hines Page">Walter Hines Page</a>, is shown the intercepted <a href="/wiki/Zimmermann_Telegram" title="Zimmermann Telegram">Zimmermann Telegram</a>, in which Germany offers to give the American Southwest back to Mexico if Mexico declares war on the United States.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg/200px-USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg" width="200" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg/300px-USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg/400px-USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1185" data-file-height="867" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:USA_bryter_de_diplomatiska_f%C3%B6rbindelserna_med_Tyskland_3_februari_1917.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
President Woodrow Wilson of the United States announces to Congress the breaking of diplomatic relations with Germany</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/March_1917" title="March 1917">March 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_1" title="March 1">March 1</a>
<ul>
<li>The U.S. government releases the text of the <a href="/wiki/Zimmermann_Telegram" title="Zimmermann Telegram">Zimmermann Telegram</a> to the public.</li>
<li>Japanese city of <a href="/wiki/%C5%8Cmuta,_Fukuoka" title="Ōmuta, Fukuoka">Ōmuta</a> is founded by Hiroushi Miruku.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_2" title="March 2">March 2</a> – The enactment of the <a href="/wiki/Jones%E2%80%93Shafroth_Act" title="Jones–Shafroth Act">Jones Act</a> grants <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Ricans</a> United States citizenship.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_4" title="March 4">March 4</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Woodrow_Wilson" title="Woodrow Wilson">Woodrow Wilson</a> is <a href="/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Woodrow_Wilson" title="Second inauguration of Woodrow Wilson">sworn in</a> for a second term as President of the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jeannette_Rankin" title="Jeannette Rankin">Jeannette Rankin</a> of <a href="/wiki/Montana" title="Montana">Montana</a> becomes the first woman member of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_7" title="March 7">March 7</a> – "<a href="/wiki/Livery_Stable_Blues" title="Livery Stable Blues">Livery Stable Blues</a>", recorded with "Dixie Jazz Band One Step" on February 26 by the <a href="/wiki/Original_Dixieland_Jass_Band" title="Original Dixieland Jass Band">Original Dixieland Jass Band</a> in the United States, becomes the first <a href="/wiki/Jazz" title="Jazz">jazz</a> recording commercially released. On August 17 the band records "<a href="/wiki/Tiger_Rag" title="Tiger Rag">Tiger Rag</a>".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_8" title="March 8">March 8</a></li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d,_1917.03.08.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d%2C_1917.03.08.jpg/220px-N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d%2C_1917.03.08.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d%2C_1917.03.08.jpg/330px-N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d%2C_1917.03.08.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d%2C_1917.03.08.jpg/440px-N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d%2C_1917.03.08.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="683" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:N%C5%91nap_-_Petrogr%C3%A1d,_1917.03.08.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Women calling for bread and peace - Petrograd, 8th of March, 1917</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li>
<ul>
<li>(N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/February_23" title="February 23">February 23</a>, O.S.) – The <a href="/wiki/February_Revolution" title="February Revolution">February Revolution</a> begins in Russia: Women calling for bread in <a href="/wiki/Petrograd" class="mw-redirect" title="Petrograd">Petrograd</a> start riots, which spontaneously spread throughout the city.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> adopts the <a href="/wiki/Cloture" title="Cloture">cloture</a> rule in order to limit <a href="/wiki/Filibuster" title="Filibuster">filibusters</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_10" title="March 10">March 10</a> – The Province of <a href="/wiki/Batangas" title="Batangas">Batangas</a> is formally founded as one of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>' first <a href="/wiki/Encomienda" title="Encomienda">encomiendas</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_11" title="March 11">March 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Revolution" title="Mexican Revolution">Mexican Revolution</a>: <a href="/wiki/Venustiano_Carranza" title="Venustiano Carranza">Venustiano Carranza</a> is elected president of Mexico; the United States gives <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> recognition of his government.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_12" title="March 12">March 12</a> – The Russian <a href="/wiki/Duma" title="Duma">Duma</a> declares a <a href="/wiki/Russian_Provisional_Government" title="Russian Provisional Government">Provisional Government</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_14" title="March 14">March 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912%E2%80%9349)" title="Republic of China (1912–49)">Republic of China</a> terminates diplomatic relations with Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_15" title="March 15">March 15</a> (N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/March_2" title="March 2">March 2</a>, O.S.) – Emperor <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_II_of_Russia" title="Nicholas II of Russia">Nicholas II of Russia</a> abdicates his throne and his son's claims. This is considered to be the end of the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russian Empire</a> after 196 years.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_16" title="March 16">March 16</a> (N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/March_3" title="March 3">March 3</a>, O.S.) – <a href="/wiki/Grand_Duke_Michael_Alexandrovich_of_Russia" title="Grand Duke Michael Alexandrovich of Russia">Grand Duke Michael Alexandrovich of Russia</a> refuses the throne, and power passes to the newly formed Provisional Government under Prince <a href="/wiki/Georgy_Lvov" title="Georgy Lvov">Georgy Lvov</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_25" title="March 25">March 25</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Georgian_Orthodox_Church" title="Georgian Orthodox Church">Georgian Orthodox Church</a> restores the <a href="/wiki/Autocephaly" title="Autocephaly">autocephaly</a> abolished by Imperial Russia in <a href="/wiki/1811" title="1811">1811</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_26" title="March 26">March 26</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/First_Battle_of_Gaza" title="First Battle of Gaza">First Battle of Gaza</a>: British <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> troops virtually encircle the Gaza garrison but are then ordered to withdraw, leaving the city to the Ottoman defenders.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_30" title="March 30">March 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hjalmar_Hammarskj%C3%B6ld" title="Hjalmar Hammarskjöld">Hjalmar Hammarskjöld</a> steps down as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Sweden" title="Prime Minister of Sweden">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>. He is replaced by the right-wing businessman and politician <a href="/wiki/Carl_Swartz" title="Carl Swartz">Carl Swartz</a> .</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_31" title="March 31">March 31</a> – The United States takes possession of the Danish West Indies, which become the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">US Virgin Islands</a>, after paying $25 million to Denmark.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/April_1917" title="April 1917">April 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_2" title="April 2">April 2</a> – WWI: U.S. President Woodrow Wilson asks the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> for a <a href="/wiki/Declaration_of_war" title="Declaration of war">declaration of war</a> on Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_6" title="April 6">April 6</a> – WWI: The United States <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Woodrow_Wilson_declares_war_on_Germany" class="extiw" title="s:Woodrow Wilson declares war on Germany">declares war on Germany</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_8" title="April 8">April 8</a> (N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/March_26" title="March 26">March 26</a>, O.S.) – In <a href="/wiki/Petrograd" class="mw-redirect" title="Petrograd">Petrograd</a>, 40,000 ethnic <a href="/wiki/Estonians" title="Estonians">Estonians</a> demand <a href="/wiki/National_autonomy" class="mw-redirect" title="National autonomy">national autonomy</a> within <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_9" title="April 9">April 9</a>–<a href="/wiki/May_16" title="May 16">May 16</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Arras_(1917)" title="Battle of Arras (1917)">Battle of Arras</a> – British Empire troops make a significant advance on the Western Front but are unable to achieve a breakthrough.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_9" title="April 9">April 9</a>–<a href="/wiki/April_12" title="April 12">12</a> – WWI: Canadian troops win the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Vimy_Ridge" title="Battle of Vimy Ridge">Battle of Vimy Ridge</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_10" title="April 10">April 10</a> – An ammunition factory explosion in <a href="/wiki/Chester,_Pennsylvania" title="Chester, Pennsylvania">Chester, Pennsylvania</a> kills 133.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_11" title="April 11">April 11</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/First_Brazilian_Republic" title="First Brazilian Republic">Brazil</a> severs diplomatic relations with Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_12" title="April 12">April 12</a> (N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/March_30" title="March 30">March 30</a> O.S.) – The <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Governorate_of_Estonia" title="Autonomous Governorate of Estonia">Autonomous Governorate of Estonia</a> is formed within <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Governorate_of_Estonia" title="Governorate of Estonia">Governorate of Estonia</a> and the northern part of the <a href="/wiki/Governorate_of_Livonia" title="Governorate of Livonia">Governorate of Livonia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_16" title="April 16">April 16</a>
<ul>
<li>(N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/April_3" title="April 3">April 3</a>, O.S.) – <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Vladimir Lenin</a> arrives at the <a href="/wiki/Finland_Station" title="Finland Station">Finland Station</a> in <a href="/wiki/Petrograd" class="mw-redirect" title="Petrograd">Petrograd</a>.</li>
<li>WWI: The <a href="/wiki/Nivelle_Offensive" title="Nivelle Offensive">Nivelle Offensive</a> commences.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lenin.gif" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/Lenin.gif/150px-Lenin.gif" width="150" height="113" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f1/Lenin.gif 1.5x" data-file-width="160" data-file-height="120" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lenin.gif" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Lenin</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_17" title="April 17">April 17</a>
<ul>
<li>(N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/April_4" title="April 4">April 4</a>, O.S.) – <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Vladimir Lenin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/April_Theses" title="April Theses">April Theses</a> are published.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> They become very influential in the following <a href="/wiki/July_Days" title="July Days">July Days</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bolshevik_Revolution" class="mw-redirect" title="Bolshevik Revolution">Bolshevik Revolution</a>.</li>
<li>WWI: The Egyptian Expeditionary Force begins the <a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Gaza" title="Second Battle of Gaza">Second Battle of Gaza</a>. This unsuccessful frontal attack on strong <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman</a> defences along with the first battle, resulted in 10,000 casualties, the dismissal of the force commander General <a href="/wiki/Archibald_Murray" title="Archibald Murray">Archibald Murray</a> and the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/Stalemate_in_Southern_Palestine" title="Stalemate in Southern Palestine">Stalemate in Southern Palestine</a>.</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Times" title="The Times">The Times</a></i> and the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mail" title="Daily Mail">Daily Mail</a></i> (London newspapers both owned by <a href="/wiki/Alfred_Harmsworth,_1st_Viscount_Northcliffe" title="Alfred Harmsworth, 1st Viscount Northcliffe">Lord Northcliffe</a>) print <a href="/wiki/Atrocity_propaganda" title="Atrocity propaganda">atrocity propaganda</a> of the supposed existence of a <a href="/wiki/German_Corpse_Factory" title="German Corpse Factory">German Corpse Factory</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_26" title="April 26">April 26</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Agreement_of_Saint-Jean-de-Maurienne" title="Agreement of Saint-Jean-de-Maurienne">Agreement of Saint-Jean-de-Maurienne</a> between France, Italy and the United Kingdom to settle interests in the Middle Eastern signed.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/May_1917" title="May 1917">May 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_9" title="May 9">May 9</a> – WWI: The <a href="/wiki/Nivelle_Offensive" title="Nivelle Offensive">Nivelle Offensive</a> is abandoned.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_13" title="May 13">May 13</a> – The nuncio Eugenio Pacelli, the future <a href="/wiki/Pope_Pius_XII" title="Pope Pius XII">Pope Pius XII</a>, is consecrated <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XV" title="Pope Benedict XV">Pope Benedict XV</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_13" title="May 13">May 13</a>–<a href="/wiki/October_13" title="October 13">October 13</a> (at monthly intervals) – 10-year-old <a href="/wiki/L%C3%BAcia_Santos" class="mw-redirect" title="Lúcia Santos">Lúcia Santos</a> and her cousins Francisco and Jacinta Marto report experiencing a series of <a href="/wiki/Marian_apparition" title="Marian apparition">Marian apparitions</a> near <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A1tima,_Portugal" title="Fátima, Portugal">Fátima, Portugal</a>, which become known as <a href="/wiki/Our_Lady_of_F%C3%A1tima" title="Our Lady of Fátima">Our Lady of Fátima</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_15" title="May 15">May 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Robert_Nivelle" title="Robert Nivelle">Robert Nivelle</a> is replaced as Commander-in-Chief of the <a href="/wiki/French_Army_in_World_War_I" title="French Army in World War I">French Army</a> by <a href="/wiki/Philippe_P%C3%A9tain" title="Philippe Pétain">Philippe Pétain</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_18" title="May 18">May 18</a> – WWI: The <a href="/wiki/Selective_Service_Act_of_1917" title="Selective Service Act of 1917">Selective Service Act</a> passes the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a>, giving the <a href="/wiki/President" title="President">President</a> the power of <a href="/wiki/Conscription" title="Conscription">conscription</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_21" title="May 21">May 21</a> – Over 300 acres (73 blocks) are destroyed in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Atlanta_fire_of_1917" title="Great Atlanta fire of 1917">Great Atlanta fire of 1917</a> in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_22" title="May 22">May 22</a>
<ul>
<li>Commissioned Officer Corps of the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Coast_and_Geodetic_Survey" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Coast and Geodetic Survey">U.S. Coast and Geodetic Survey</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lynching_of_Ell_Persons" title="Lynching of Ell Persons">Ell Persons</a> is lynched in Memphis in connection with the rape and murder of 16-year-old Antoinette Rappal.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_23" title="May 23">May 23</a>
<ul>
<li>A month of civil violence in <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a>, Italy, ends after the Italian army forcibly takes over the city from anarchists and anti-war revolutionaries. Fifty people are killed and 800 arrested.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li>WWI: During the <a href="/wiki/Stalemate_in_Southern_Palestine" title="Stalemate in Southern Palestine">Stalemate in Southern Palestine</a> the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_the_Beersheba_to_Hafir_el_Auja_railway" title="Raid on the Beersheba to Hafir el Auja railway">Raid on the Beersheba to Hafir el Auja railway</a> by <a href="/wiki/Desert_Column" title="Desert Column">Desert Column</a> of British Empire troops, destroys large sections of the railway line linking <a href="/wiki/Beersheba" title="Beersheba">Beersheba</a> to the main <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Ottoman Army">Ottoman</a> desert base.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_26" title="May 26">May 26</a> – A <a href="/wiki/May%E2%80%93June_1917_tornado_outbreak_sequence" title="May–June 1917 tornado outbreak sequence">tornado</a> strikes <a href="/wiki/Mattoon,_Illinois" title="Mattoon, Illinois">Mattoon, Illinois</a>, causing devastation and killing 101 people.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_27" title="May 27">May 27</a> – WWI: Over 30,000 French troops refuse to go to the trenches at <a href="/wiki/Missy-aux-Bois" title="Missy-aux-Bois">Missy-aux-Bois</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_27" title="May 27">May 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XV" title="Pope Benedict XV">Pope Benedict XV</a> <a href="/wiki/Promulgation_(canon_law)" title="Promulgation (canon law)">promulgates</a> the <a href="/wiki/1917_Code_of_Canon_Law" title="1917 Code of Canon Law">1917 Code of Canon Law</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/June_1917" title="June 1917">June 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a> – <a href="/wiki/French_Army_Mutinies" class="mw-redirect" title="French Army Mutinies">French Army Mutinies</a>: A French infantry regiment seizes <a href="/wiki/Missy-aux-Bois" title="Missy-aux-Bois">Missy-aux-Bois</a> and declares an anti-war military government. Other French army troops soon apprehend them.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_4" title="June 4">June 4</a> – The first <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer Prizes</a> are awarded: <a href="/wiki/Laura_E._Richards" title="Laura E. Richards">Laura E. Richards</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maud_Howe_Elliott" title="Maud Howe Elliott">Maud Howe Elliott</a> and <a href="/wiki/Florence_Hall_(Pulitzer_Prize_winner)" title="Florence Hall (Pulitzer Prize winner)">Florence Hall</a> receive the first <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer</a> for a biography (for <i><a href="/wiki/Julia_Ward_Howe" title="Julia Ward Howe">Julia Ward Howe</a></i>). <a href="/wiki/Jean_Jules_Jusserand" title="Jean Jules Jusserand">Jean Jules Jusserand</a> receives the first <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer</a> for history for his work <i>With Americans of Past and Present Days.</i> <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Bayard_Swope" title="Herbert Bayard Swope">Herbert Bayard Swope</a> receives the first <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer</a> for journalism for his work for the <i><a href="/wiki/New_York_World" title="New York World">New York World</a>.</i></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_5" title="June 5">June 5</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Conscription" title="Conscription">Conscription</a> begins in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_7" title="June 7">June 7</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Messines_(1917)" title="Battle of Messines (1917)">Battle of Messines</a> opens with the British Army detonating 19 <a href="/wiki/Ammonal" title="Ammonal">ammonal</a> <a href="/wiki/Mining_(military)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mining (military)">mines</a> under the German lines, killing 10,000 in the deadliest deliberate non-nuclear man-made explosion in history.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_8" title="June 8">June 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Speculator_Mine_disaster" title="Speculator Mine disaster">Speculator Mine disaster</a>: A fire at the Granite Mountain and Speculator ore mine outside <a href="/wiki/Butte,_Montana" title="Butte, Montana">Butte, Montana</a> kills at least 168 workers.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_11" title="June 11">June 11</a> – King <a href="/wiki/Constantine_I_of_Greece" title="Constantine I of Greece">Constantine I of Greece</a> abdicates for the first time, being succeeded by his son <a href="/wiki/Alexander_of_Greece" title="Alexander of Greece">Alexander</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_13" title="June 13">June 13</a> – WWI: The first major German bombing raid on London by fixed-wing aircraft leaves 162 dead and 432 injured.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_15" title="June 15">June 15</a> – The United States enacts the <a href="/wiki/Espionage_Act_of_1917" title="Espionage Act of 1917">Espionage Act</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/July_1917" title="July 1917">July 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li>July – First <a href="/wiki/Cottingley_Fairies" title="Cottingley Fairies">Cottingley Fairies</a> photographs taken in <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire" title="Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a>, England, apparently depicting fairies; a hoax not admitted by the child creators until 1981.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_1" title="July 1">July 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/East_St._Louis_riot" class="mw-redirect" title="East St. Louis riot">East St. Louis riot</a>: A labor dispute ignites a <a href="/wiki/Race_riot" class="mw-redirect" title="Race riot">race riot</a> in <a href="/wiki/East_St._Louis,_Illinois" title="East St. Louis, Illinois">East St. Louis, Illinois</a>, which leaves 250 dead.</li>
<li>Russian General <a href="/wiki/Brusilov" title="Brusilov">Brusilov</a> begins the major <a href="/wiki/Kerensky_Offensive" title="Kerensky Offensive">Kerensky Offensive</a> in <a href="/wiki/Galicia_(Eastern_Europe)" title="Galicia (Eastern Europe)">Galicia</a>, initially advancing towards <a href="/wiki/Lemberg" class="mw-redirect" title="Lemberg">Lemberg</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_2" title="July 2">July 2</a> – WWI: Greece joins the war on the side of the <a href="/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_I" title="Allies of World War I">Allies</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_6" title="July 6">July 6</a> – WWI:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Aqaba" title="Battle of Aqaba">Battle of Aqaba</a>: <a href="/wiki/Arab_Revolt" title="Arab Revolt">Arabian troops</a> led by <a href="/wiki/T._E._Lawrence" title="T. E. Lawrence">T. E. Lawrence</a> capture <a href="/wiki/Aqaba" title="Aqaba">Aqaba</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman Empire</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Conscription_Crisis_of_1917" title="Conscription Crisis of 1917">Conscription Crisis of 1917</a> in Canada leads to passage of the Military Service Act.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_7" title="July 7">July 7</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Lions_Clubs_International" title="Lions Clubs International">Lions Clubs International</a> is formed in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_8" title="July 8">July 8</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_13" title="July 13">13</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battles_of_Ramadi_(1917)#First_Battle_of_Ramadi" title="Battles of Ramadi (1917)">First Battle of Ramadi</a>: British troops fail to take <a href="/wiki/Ramadi" title="Ramadi">Ramadi</a> from the Ottoman Empire; a majority of British casualties are due to extreme heat.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_12" title="July 12">July 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bisbee_Deportation" title="Bisbee Deportation">Bisbee Deportation</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Phelps_Dodge" title="Phelps Dodge">Phelps Dodge</a> Corporation deports over 1,000 suspected <a href="/wiki/Industrial_Workers_of_the_World" title="Industrial Workers of the World">IWW</a> members from <a href="/wiki/Bisbee,_Arizona" title="Bisbee, Arizona">Bisbee, Arizona</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_16" title="July 16">July 16</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_17" title="July 17">July 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russian</a> troops mutiny, abandon the <a href="/wiki/Austria-Hungary" title="Austria-Hungary">Austrian</a> front, and retreat to the <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>; hundreds are shot by their commanding officers during the retreat.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_16" title="July 16">July 16</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_18" title="July 18">July 18</a> – Serious clashes in <a href="/wiki/Petrograd" class="mw-redirect" title="Petrograd">Petrograd</a> in <a href="/wiki/July_Days" title="July Days">July Days</a>; <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Lenin</a> escapes to <a href="/wiki/Grand_Principality_of_Finland" class="mw-redirect" title="Grand Principality of Finland">Finland</a>; <a href="/wiki/Leon_Trotsky" title="Leon Trotsky">Trotsky</a> is arrested.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_17" title="July 17">July 17</a> – King <a href="/wiki/George_V" title="George V">George V</a> of the United Kingdom issues a proclamation, stating that thenceforth the male line descendants of the <a href="/wiki/British_Royal_Family" class="mw-redirect" title="British Royal Family">British Royal Family</a> will bear the surname <a href="/wiki/House_of_Windsor" title="House of Windsor">Windsor</a>, vice the Germanic bloodline of <i><a href="/wiki/House_of_Saxe-Coburg_and_Gotha" title="House of Saxe-Coburg and Gotha">House of Saxe-Coburg and Gotha</a></i>, which is an offshoot of the historic (800+ years) <a href="/wiki/House_of_Wettin" title="House of Wettin">House of Wettin</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_20" title="July 20">July 20</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Finland" title="Parliament of Finland">Parliament of Finland</a>, with a <a href="/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Finland" title="Social Democratic Party of Finland">Social Democratic</a> majority, passes a "Sovereignty Act", declaring itself, as the representative of the Finnish people, sovereign over the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Principality_of_Finland" class="mw-redirect" title="Grand Principality of Finland">Grand Principality of Finland</a>. The Russian Provisional Government does not recognize the act, as it would have devolved Russian sovereignty over Finland, formerly exercised by the Russian Emperor as Grand Prince of Finland and alter the relationship between Finland and Russia into a real union with Russia solely responsible for the defence and foreign relations of an independent Finland.</li>
<li>(<a href="/wiki/July_7" title="July 7">July 7</a>, O.S.) – <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Kerensky" title="Alexander Kerensky">Alexander Kerensky</a> becomes <a href="/wiki/Premier" title="Premier">premier</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Provisional_Government" title="Russian Provisional Government">Russian Provisional Government</a>, replacing Prince <a href="/wiki/Georgy_Lvov" title="Georgy Lvov">Georgy Lvov</a>.</li>
<li>The Russian Provisional Government enacts <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_suffrage" title="Women's suffrage">women's suffrage</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Corfu_Declaration" title="Corfu Declaration">Corfu Declaration</a>, which enables the establishment of the post-war <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Yugoslavia" title="Kingdom of Yugoslavia">Kingdom of Yugoslavia</a>, is signed by the <a href="/wiki/Yugoslav_Committee" title="Yugoslav Committee">Yugoslav Committee</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Serbia" title="Kingdom of Serbia">Kingdom of Serbia</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_20" title="July 20">July 20</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_28" title="July 28">July 28</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Austria-Hungary" title="Austria-Hungary">Austrian</a> and <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">German</a> forces repulse the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">Russian</a> advance into <a href="/wiki/Galicia_(Eastern_Europe)" title="Galicia (Eastern Europe)">Galicia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_25" title="July 25">July 25</a> – Sir <a href="/wiki/William_Thomas_White" title="William Thomas White">William Thomas White</a> introduces Canada's first <a href="/wiki/Income_tax" title="Income tax">income tax</a> as a "temporary" measure (lowest bracket is 4% and highest is 25%).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_28" title="July 28">July 28</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Silent_Parade" title="Silent Parade">Silent Parade</a> is organized by the <a href="/wiki/NAACP" class="mw-redirect" title="NAACP">NAACP</a> in New York City to protest the <a href="/wiki/East_St._Louis_riot" class="mw-redirect" title="East St. Louis riot">East St. Louis riot</a> of <a href="/wiki/July_2" title="July 2">July 2</a>, as well as lynchings in <a href="/wiki/Tennessee" title="Tennessee">Tennessee</a> and <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_30" title="July 30">July 30</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Finland" title="Parliament of Finland">Parliament of Finland</a> is dissolved by the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Provisional_Government" title="Russian Provisional Government">Russian Provisional Government</a>. New elections are held in the autumn, resulting in a bourgeois majority.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_31" title="July 31">July 31</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Passchendaele" title="Battle of Passchendaele">Battle of Passchendaele</a> ("Third Battle of Ypres"): Allied offensive operations commence in Flanders.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/August_1917" title="August 1917">August 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li>August – The <a href="/wiki/Green_Corn_Rebellion" title="Green Corn Rebellion">Green Corn Rebellion</a>, an uprising by several hundred farmers against the WWI draft, takes place in central <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_2" title="August 2">August 2</a> – <a href="/wiki/Edwin_Harris_Dunning" title="Edwin Harris Dunning">Squadron Commander E.H. Dunning</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20060628134612/http://www.royal-navy.mod.uk/server/show/nav.3919">lands his aircraft on the ship</a> <a href="/wiki/HMS_Furious_(47)" title="HMS Furious (47)">HMS&#160;<i>Furious</i></a> in <a href="/wiki/Scapa_Flow" title="Scapa Flow">Scapa Flow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Orkney" title="Orkney">Orkney</a>. He is killed 5 days later during another landing on the ship.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_3" title="August 3">August 3</a> – The <a href="/wiki/New_York_Guard" title="New York Guard">New York Guard</a> is founded.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_10" title="August 10">August 10</a> – A general strike begins in Spain; it is smashed after 3 days with 70 left dead, hundreds of wounded and 2,000 arrests.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_14" title="August 14">August 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912%E2%80%9349)" title="Republic of China (1912–49)">Republic of China</a> declares war on Germany and Austria-Hungary.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_17" title="August 17">August 17</a> – One of English literature's important meetings takes place when <a href="/wiki/Wilfred_Owen" title="Wilfred Owen">Wilfred Owen</a> introduces himself to <a href="/wiki/Siegfried_Sassoon" title="Siegfried Sassoon">Siegfried Sassoon</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Craiglockhart_War_Hospital" class="mw-redirect" title="Craiglockhart War Hospital">Craiglockhart War Hospital</a> in <a href="/wiki/Edinburgh" title="Edinburgh">Edinburgh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_18" title="August 18">August 18</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Great_Thessaloniki_Fire_of_1917" title="Great Thessaloniki Fire of 1917">Great Thessaloniki Fire of 1917</a> in Greece destroys 32% of the city, leaving 70,000 individuals homeless.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_29" title="August 29">August 29</a> – WWI: The <a href="/wiki/Military_Service_Act_(Canada)" title="Military Service Act (Canada)">Military Service Act</a> is passed in the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_House_of_Commons" class="mw-redirect" title="Canadian House of Commons">Canadian House of Commons</a>, giving the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Canada" title="Government of Canada">Government of Canada</a> the right to conscript men into the army.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/September_1917" title="September 1917">September 1917</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_14" title="September 14">September 14</a> – Russia is declared a <a href="/wiki/Russian_Republic" title="Russian Republic">republic</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Provisional_Government" title="Russian Provisional Government">Provisional Government</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_23" title="September 23">September 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Leon_Trotsky" title="Leon Trotsky">Leon Trotsky</a> is elected Chairman of the <a href="/wiki/Petrograd_Soviet" title="Petrograd Soviet">Petrograd Soviet</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_25" title="September 25">September 25</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Mossovet" title="Mossovet">Mossovet</a> (<a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> Soviet of People's Deputies) votes to side with the <a href="/wiki/Bolsheviks" title="Bolsheviks">Bolsheviks</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_26" title="September 26">September 26</a>–<a href="/wiki/October_3" title="October 3">October 3</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Polygon_Wood" title="Battle of Polygon Wood">Battle of Polygon Wood</a> (part of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Passchendaele" title="Battle of Passchendaele">Battle of Passchendaele</a>) near <a href="/wiki/Ypres" title="Ypres">Ypres</a> in Belgium: British and Australian troops capture positions from the Germans.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_28" title="September 28">September 28</a>–<a href="/wiki/September_29" title="September 29">29</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battles_of_Ramadi_(1917)#Second_Battle_of_Ramadi" title="Battles of Ramadi (1917)">Second Battle of Ramadi</a>: British troops take <a href="/wiki/Ramadi" title="Ramadi">Ramadi</a> from the Ottoman Empire.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_4" title="October 4">October 4</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Broodseinde" title="Battle of Broodseinde">Battle of Broodseinde</a> near Ypres: British Imperial forces overpower the <a href="/wiki/4th_Army_(German_Empire)" title="4th Army (German Empire)">German 4th Army</a>'s defences.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_12" title="October 12">October 12</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/First_Battle_of_Passchendaele" title="First Battle of Passchendaele">First Battle of Passchendaele</a>: Allies fail to take a German defensive position with the biggest loss of life in a single day for New Zealand, over 800 of whose men and 45 officers are killed, roughly 1 in 1000 of the nation's population at this time.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_12" title="October 12">October 12</a>-<a href="/wiki/October_19" title="October 19">19</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Operation_Albion" title="Operation Albion">Operation Albion</a>: German forces land on and capture the <a href="/wiki/West_Estonian_archipelago" title="West Estonian archipelago">West Estonian archipelago</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_13" title="October 13">October 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Miracle_of_the_Sun" title="Miracle of the Sun">Miracle of the Sun</a> at <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A1tima,_Portugal" title="Fátima, Portugal">Fátima, Portugal</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_15" title="October 15">October 15</a> – WWI: At <a href="/wiki/Vincennes" title="Vincennes">Vincennes</a> outside Paris, Dutch dancer <a href="/wiki/Mata_Hari" title="Mata Hari">Mata Hari</a> is executed by <a href="/wiki/Firing_squad" class="mw-redirect" title="Firing squad">firing squad</a> for <a href="/wiki/Espionage" title="Espionage">spying</a> for Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_19" title="October 19">October 19</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dallas_Love_Field" title="Dallas Love Field">Dallas Love Field</a> airport is opened.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carl_Swartz" title="Carl Swartz">Carl Swartz</a> leaves office as Prime Minister of Sweden after dismal election results for the right-wing in the Riksdag elections in September. He is replaced by liberal leader and history professor <a href="/wiki/Nils_Ed%C3%A9n" title="Nils Edén">Nils Edén</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Brazil_during_World_War_I" title="Brazil during World War I">Brazilian</a> ship is destroyed by a German U-Boat, encouraging Brazil to enter World War I.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_25" title="October 25">October 25</a> (O.S.) (<a href="/wiki/November_7" title="November 7">November 7</a>, N.S.) – Traditional beginning date of the <a href="/wiki/October_Revolution" title="October Revolution">October Revolution</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russian_Civil_War" title="Russian Civil War">Russian Civil War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_26" title="October 26">October 26</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> <a href="/wiki/First_Brazilian_Republic#Brazil_in_World_War_I" title="First Brazilian Republic">declares war</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Central_Powers" title="Central Powers">Central Powers</a>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg/220px-Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg" width="220" height="140" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg/330px-Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg/440px-Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg 2x" data-file-width="606" data-file-height="385" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s_declara_guerra_1917.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Brazilian President <a href="/wiki/Venceslau_Br%C3%A1s" title="Venceslau Brás">Venceslau Brás</a> signs a declaration of war against the <a href="/wiki/Central_Powers" title="Central Powers">Central Powers</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_27" title="October 27">October 27</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman</a> force attacks <a href="/wiki/Desert_Mounted_Corps" title="Desert Mounted Corps">Desert Mounted Corps</a> units garrisoning el Buqqar ridge during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Buqqar_Ridge" title="Battle of Buqqar Ridge">Battle of Buqqar Ridge</a> fought in the last days of the <a href="/wiki/Stalemate_in_Southern_Palestine" title="Stalemate in Southern Palestine">Stalemate in Southern Palestine</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_31" title="October 31">October 31</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Beersheba_(1917)" title="Battle of Beersheba (1917)">Battle of Beersheba</a>: The British <a href="/wiki/XX_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XX Corps (United Kingdom)">XX Corps</a> and <a href="/wiki/Desert_Mounted_Corps" title="Desert Mounted Corps">Desert Mounted Corps</a> (<a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a>) attack and capture <a href="/wiki/Beersheba" title="Beersheba">Beersheba</a> ending the <a href="/wiki/Stalemate_in_Southern_Palestine" title="Stalemate in Southern Palestine">Stalemate in Southern Palestine</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_1" title="November 1">November 1</a> – WWI:
<ul>
<li>The British <a href="/wiki/XXI_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XXI Corps (United Kingdom)">XXI Corps</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> begins the <a href="/wiki/Third_Battle_of_Gaza" title="Third Battle of Gaza">Third Battle of Gaza</a>.</li>
<li>The British <a href="/wiki/Desert_Mounted_Corps" title="Desert Mounted Corps">Desert Mounted Corps</a> begins the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Tel_el_Khuweilfe" title="Battle of Tel el Khuweilfe">Battle of Tel el Khuweilfe</a> in the direction of <a href="/wiki/Hebron" title="Hebron">Hebron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_2" title="November 2">November 2</a> – <a href="/wiki/Zionism" title="Zionism">Zionism</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_Foreign_and_Commonwealth_Affairs" title="Secretary of State for Foreign and Commonwealth Affairs">British Foreign Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Balfour" title="Arthur Balfour">Arthur Balfour</a> makes the <a href="/wiki/Balfour_Declaration" title="Balfour Declaration">Balfour Declaration</a> proclaiming British support for the "establishment in <a href="/wiki/Palestine_(region)" title="Palestine (region)">Palestine</a> of a national home for the Jewish people" with the clear understanding "that nothing shall be done which may prejudice the civil and religious rights of existing non-Jewish communities".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_5" title="November 5">November 5</a> (N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a>, O.S.) – Estonian and Russian Bolsheviks seize power in <a href="/wiki/Tallinn" title="Tallinn">Tallinn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Governorate_of_Estonia" title="Autonomous Governorate of Estonia">Autonomous Governorate of Estonia</a>, two days before the <a href="/wiki/October_Revolution" title="October Revolution">October Revolution</a> in <a href="/wiki/Petrograd" class="mw-redirect" title="Petrograd">Petrograd</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_6" title="November 6">November 6</a>
<ul>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Passchendaele" title="Second Battle of Passchendaele">Second Battle of Passchendaele</a>: After 3 months of fierce fighting, Canadian forces take <a href="/wiki/Passendale" title="Passendale">Passchendaele</a> in Belgium. The battle concludes on November 10.</li>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hareira_and_Sheria" title="Battle of Hareira and Sheria">Battle of Hareira and Sheria</a> launched by the British <a href="/wiki/XX_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XX Corps (United Kingdom)">XX Corps</a> and <a href="/wiki/Desert_Mounted_Corps" title="Desert Mounted Corps">Desert Mounted Corps</a> against the central <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Ottoman Army">Ottoman</a> defences protecting the Gaza to Beersheba road.</li>
<li>Militants from Trotsky's committee join with trusty Bolshevik soldiers to seize government buildings and pounce on members of the provisional government.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_7" title="November 7">November 7</a>
<ul>
<li>(N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/October_25" title="October 25">October 25</a>, O.S.) – <a href="/wiki/October_Revolution" title="October Revolution">October Revolution</a> in Russia: The workers of the <a href="/wiki/St._Petersburg" class="mw-redirect" title="St. Petersburg">Petrograd</a> <a href="/wiki/Workers%27_council" title="Workers' council">Soviet</a> in Russia, led by the <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Communist Party of the Soviet Union">Bolshevik Party</a> and leader <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Vladimir Lenin</a>, storm the <a href="/wiki/Winter_Palace" title="Winter Palace">Winter Palace</a> and successfully destroy the <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Kerensky" title="Alexander Kerensky">Kerensky</a> <a href="/wiki/Russian_Provisional_Government" title="Russian Provisional Government">Provisional Government</a> after less than eight months of rule. This immediately, triggers the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Civil_War" title="Russian Civil War">Russian Civil War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/History_of_Iran" title="History of Iran">Iran</a> (which has provided weapons for Russia) refuses to support the <a href="/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_II" title="Allies of World War II">Allied Forces</a> after the <a href="/wiki/October_Revolution" title="October Revolution">October Revolution</a>.</li>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Third_Battle_of_Gaza" title="Third Battle of Gaza">Third Battle of Gaza</a>: <a href="/wiki/XXI_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XXI Corps (United Kingdom)">XXI Corps</a> occupies <a href="/wiki/Gaza_City" title="Gaza City">Gaza</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Ottoman Army">Ottoman</a> garrison withdraws.</li>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hareira_and_Sheria" title="Battle of Hareira and Sheria">Battle of Hareira and Sheria</a> continues when the <a href="/wiki/XX_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XX Corps (United Kingdom)">XX Corps</a> and <a href="/wiki/Desert_Mounted_Corps" title="Desert Mounted Corps">Desert Mounted Corps</a> capture Hareira and Sheria, marking the end of the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman</a> Gaza to Beersheba line.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Women%27s_suffrage_in_the_United_States" title="Women's suffrage in the United States">Women's Suffrage in the United States</a>: Women won the right to vote in New York State.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_13" title="November 13">November 13</a> – WWI:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> attack retreating <a href="/wiki/Yildirim_Army_Group" title="Yildirim Army Group">Yildirim Army Group</a> forces during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Mughar_Ridge" title="Battle of Mughar Ridge">Battle of Mughar Ridge</a> results in the capture of 10,000 <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Ottoman Army">Ottoman</a> prisoners, 100 guns and 50 miles (80&#160;km) of <a href="/wiki/Palestine_(region)" title="Palestine (region)">Palestine</a> territory.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ANZAC_Mounted_Division" title="ANZAC Mounted Division">ANZAC Mounted Division</a> (<a href="/wiki/Desert_Mounted_Corps" title="Desert Mounted Corps">Desert Mounted Corps</a>) successfully fights the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Ayun_Kara" title="Battle of Ayun Kara">Battle of Ayun Kara</a> in the aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Mughar_Ridge" title="Battle of Mughar Ridge">Battle of Mughar Ridge</a> against strong <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">German</a> rearguards.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_15" title="November 15">November 15</a>
<ul>
<li>In a "Night of Terror" in the United States, influential suffragettes from the <a href="/wiki/Silent_Sentinels" title="Silent Sentinels">Silent Sentinels</a> are deliberately subjected to physical assaults by guards while imprisoned.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Finland" title="Parliament of Finland">Parliament of Finland</a> passes another "Sovereignty Act", dissolving Russian sovereignty over Finland and effectively declaring Finland independent.</li>
<li>(N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/November_28" title="November 28">November 28</a>, O.S.) – The <a href="/wiki/Estonian_Provincial_Assembly" class="mw-redirect" title="Estonian Provincial Assembly">Provincial Assembly</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Governorate_of_Estonia" title="Autonomous Governorate of Estonia">Autonomous Governorate of Estonia</a> declares itself the highest legal body in <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_16" title="November 16">November 16</a>
<ul>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/ANZAC_Mounted_Division" title="ANZAC Mounted Division">ANZAC Mounted Division</a> occupies <a href="/wiki/Jaffa" title="Jaffa">Jaffa</a> following their victory at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Ayun_Kara" title="Battle of Ayun Kara">Battle of Ayun Kara</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Georges_Clemenceau" title="Georges Clemenceau">Georges Clemenceau</a> becomes prime minister of France.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_17" title="November 17">November 17</a>
<ul>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Action_of_17_November_1917" title="Action of 17 November 1917">Action of 17 November 1917</a>: United States Navy <a href="/wiki/Destroyer" title="Destroyer">destroyers</a> <a href="/wiki/USS_Fanning_(DD-37)" title="USS Fanning (DD-37)">USS <i>Fanning</i></a> and <a href="/wiki/USS_Nicholson_(DD-52)" title="USS Nicholson (DD-52)">USS <i>Nicholson</i></a> capture <a href="/wiki/Imperial_German_Navy" title="Imperial German Navy">Imperial German Navy</a> <a href="/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">U-boat</a> <a href="/wiki/SM_U-58" title="SM U-58">SM <i>U-58</i></a> off the south-west coast of Ireland, the first combat action in which U.S. ships take a submarine (which is then <a href="/wiki/Scuttled" class="mw-redirect" title="Scuttled">scuttled</a>).</li>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Jerusalem_(1917)" class="mw-redirect" title="Battle of Jerusalem (1917)">Battle of Jerusalem (1917)</a> begins with the <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> launching attacks against <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Army" class="mw-redirect" title="Ottoman Army">Ottoman</a> forces in the <a href="/wiki/Judean_Hills" class="mw-redirect" title="Judean Hills">Judean Hills</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Dispensary_for_Sick_Animals" title="People's Dispensary for Sick Animals">People's Dispensary for Sick Animals</a> is founded in the United Kingdom.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_20" title="November 20">November 20</a>
<ul>
<li>WWI: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Cambrai_(1917)" title="Battle of Cambrai (1917)">Battle of Cambrai</a>: British forces, using <a href="/wiki/Tank" title="Tank">tanks</a>, make early progress in an attack on German positions but are soon beaten back.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> is declared a republic.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_22" title="November 22">November 22</a> – In <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, Quebec, Canada, the <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_Association" title="National Hockey Association">National Hockey Association</a> suspends operations.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_23" title="November 23">November 23</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Bolsheviks" title="Bolsheviks">Bolsheviks</a> release the full text of the previously secret <a href="/wiki/Sykes%E2%80%93Picot_Agreement" title="Sykes–Picot Agreement">Sykes–Picot Agreement</a> of <a href="/wiki/1916" title="1916">1916</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Izvestia" title="Izvestia">Izvestia</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Pravda" title="Pravda">Pravda</a></i>; it is printed in the <i><a href="/wiki/Manchester_Guardian" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester Guardian">Manchester Guardian</a></i> on November 26.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_24" title="November 24">November 24</a> – Nine members of the <a href="/wiki/Milwaukee_Police_Department" title="Milwaukee Police Department">Milwaukee Police Department</a> are killed by a bomb, the most deaths in a single event in U.S. police history until the <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">September 11 attacks</a> in <a href="/wiki/2001" title="2001">2001</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_25" title="November 25">November 25</a> – WWI: German forces <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Ngomano" title="Battle of Ngomano">defeat Portuguese army</a> of about 1200 at <a href="/wiki/Negomano" title="Negomano">Negomano</a> on the border of modern-day <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">Mozambique</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_26" title="November 26">November 26</a> – The <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">National Hockey League</a> is formed in Montreal as a replacement for the recently disbanded <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_Association" title="National Hockey Association">National Hockey Association</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_28" title="November 28">November 28</a> – WWI: The <a href="/wiki/Bolsheviks" title="Bolsheviks">Bolsheviks</a> offer peace terms to the <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">Germans</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>December – <a href="/wiki/Annie_Besant" title="Annie Besant">Annie Besant</a> becomes president of the <a href="/wiki/Indian_National_Congress" title="Indian National Congress">Indian National Congress</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_3" title="December 3">December 3</a> – After nearly 20 years of planning and construction, the <a href="/wiki/Quebec_Bridge" title="Quebec Bridge">Quebec Bridge</a> opens to traffic (the bridge partially collapsed on <a href="/wiki/August_29" title="August 29">August 29</a>, 1907 and <a href="/wiki/September_11" title="September 11">September 11</a>, 1916).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_6" title="December 6">December 6</a>
<ul>
<li>The Senate of Finland officially declares the country's independence from <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Halifax_Explosion" title="Halifax Explosion">Halifax Explosion</a>: Two freighters collide in <a href="/wiki/Halifax_Harbour" title="Halifax Harbour">Halifax Harbour</a> at <a href="/wiki/Halifax,_Nova_Scotia" title="Halifax, Nova Scotia">Halifax, Nova Scotia</a> and cause a huge explosion that kills at least 1,963 people, injures 9,000 and destroys part of the city (the biggest man-made explosion in recorded history until the <a href="/wiki/Trinity_(nuclear_test)" title="Trinity (nuclear test)">Trinity</a> <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapons_testing" title="Nuclear weapons testing">nuclear test</a> in 1945).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_9" title="December 9">December 9</a> – WWI: The British <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> accepts the surrender of <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a> by the mayor, <a href="/wiki/Hussein_al-Husayni" title="Hussein al-Husayni">Hussein al-Husayni</a>, following effective defeat of the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">Ottoman Empire</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Yildirim_Army_Group" title="Yildirim Army Group">Yildirim Army Group</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Jerusalem_(1917)" class="mw-redirect" title="Battle of Jerusalem (1917)">Battle of Jerusalem</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_11" title="December 11">December 11</a> – WWI: General <a href="/wiki/Edmund_Allenby" class="mw-redirect" title="Edmund Allenby">Edmund Allenby</a> leads units of the British <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> into <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a> on foot through the <a href="/wiki/Jaffa_Gate" title="Jaffa Gate">Jaffa Gate</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_17" title="December 17">December 17</a> – The <i><a href="/wiki/Raad_van_Vlaanderen_(World_War_I)" class="mw-redirect" title="Raad van Vlaanderen (World War I)">Raad van Vlaanderen</a></i> proclaims the independence of <a href="/wiki/Flanders" title="Flanders">Flanders</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_20" title="December 20">December 20</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Cheka" title="Cheka">Cheka</a>, a predecessor to the <a href="/wiki/KGB" title="KGB">KGB</a> is established in Russia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_23" title="December 23">December 23</a> (N.S.) (<a href="/wiki/February_23" title="February 23">February 23</a>, O.S.) – A local plebiscite supports transferring <a href="/wiki/Narva" title="Narva">Narva</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ivangorod" title="Ivangorod">Ivangorod</a> (<i>Jaanilinn</i>) from <a href="/wiki/Petrograd_Governorate" class="mw-redirect" title="Petrograd Governorate">Petrograd Governorate</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Governorate_of_Estonia" title="Autonomous Governorate of Estonia">Autonomous Governorate of Estonia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_25" title="December 25">December 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Jesse_Lynch_Williams" title="Jesse Lynch Williams">Jesse Lynch Williams</a>' <i><a href="/wiki/Why_Marry%3F" title="Why Marry?">Why Marry?</a></i>, the first dramatic play to win a <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer Prize</a>, opens at the <a href="/wiki/Astor_Theatre,_New_York_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Astor Theatre, New York City">Astor Theatre</a> in New York.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_26" title="December 26">December 26</a> – United States president <a href="/wiki/Woodrow_Wilson" title="Woodrow Wilson">Woodrow Wilson</a> uses the Federal Possession and Control Act to place most U.S. railroads under the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Railroad_Administration" title="United States Railroad Administration">United States Railroad Administration</a>, hoping to transport troops and materials for the war effort more efficiently.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_30" title="December 30">December 30</a> – WWI: <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Expeditionary_Force" title="Egyptian Expeditionary Force">Egyptian Expeditionary Force</a> secures the victory at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Jerusalem_(1917)#Defence_of_Jerusalem" class="mw-redirect" title="Battle of Jerusalem (1917)">Battle of Jerusalem</a> by successfully defending Jerusalem from numerous <a href="/wiki/Yildirim_Army_Group" title="Yildirim Army Group">Yildirim Army Group</a> counterattacks.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Date unknown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Following the <a href="/wiki/October_Revolution" title="October Revolution">October Revolution</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alexandra_Kollontai" title="Alexandra Kollontai">Alexandra Kollontai</a> is appointed <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Commissar" class="mw-redirect" title="People's Commissar">People's Commissar</a> for Social Welfare in the <a href="/wiki/Council_of_People%27s_Commissars" title="Council of People's Commissars">Council of People's Commissars</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_Russian_Soviet_Federative_Socialist_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="Government of the Russian Soviet Federative Socialist Republic">Government of the Russian Soviet Federative Socialist Republic</a>, the first woman <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_(government)" title="Cabinet (government)">cabinet</a> <a href="/wiki/Minister_(government)" title="Minister (government)">minister</a> in Europe.</li>
<li>Women are permitted to stand in national elections in the Netherlands.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/True_Jesus_Church" title="True Jesus Church">True Jesus Church</a> is established in Beijing.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Births">Births</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Births">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li><a href="/wiki/January_6" title="January 6">January 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Koo_Chen-fu" title="Koo Chen-fu">Koo Chen-fu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nationalist_Chinese" class="mw-redirect" title="Nationalist Chinese">Nationalist Chinese</a> negotiator (d. <a href="/wiki/2005" title="2005">2005</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_10" title="January 10">January 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/Jerry_Wexler" title="Jerry Wexler">Jerry Wexler</a>, American record producer (d. <a href="/wiki/2008" title="2008">2008</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_12" title="January 12">January 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Skinner" title="Jimmy Skinner">Jimmy Skinner</a>, Detroit Red Wings head coach (d. <a href="/wiki/2007" title="2007">2007</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_15" title="January 15">January 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/K._A._Thangavelu" title="K. A. Thangavelu">K. A. Thangavelu</a>, Indian film actor and comedian (d. <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_16" title="January 16">January 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Carl_Karcher" title="Carl Karcher">Carl Karcher</a>, American founder of the <i>Carl's Jr.</i> hamburger chain (d. <a href="/wiki/2008" title="2008">2008</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_17" title="January 17">January 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/M._G._Ramachandran" title="M. G. Ramachandran">M. G. Ramachandran</a>, Tamil Nadu chief minister and actor (d. <a href="/wiki/1987" title="1987">1987</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_19" title="January 19">January 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Graham_Higman" title="Graham Higman">Graham Higman</a>, British mathematician (d. <a href="/wiki/2008" title="2008">2008</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_21" title="January 21">January 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Erling_Persson" title="Erling Persson">Erling Persson</a>, Swedish businessman and founder of <a href="/wiki/H%26M" title="H&amp;M">H&amp;M</a> (d. <a href="/wiki/2002" title="2002">2002</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_24" title="January 24">January 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Borgnine" title="Ernest Borgnine">Ernest Borgnine</a>, American actor (d. <a href="/wiki/2012" title="2012">2012</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_25" title="January 25">January 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ilya_Prigogine" title="Ilya Prigogine">Ilya Prigogine</a>, Russian-born physicist and chemist, recipient of the <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Chemistry" title="Nobel Prize in Chemistry">Nobel Prize in Chemistry</a> (d. <a href="/wiki/2003" title="2003">2003</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_26" title="January 26">January 26</a>
<ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/William_Verity_Jr." title="William Verity Jr.">William Verity Jr.</a>, American politician (d. <a href="/wiki/2007" title="2007">2007</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>

</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/September_15" title="September 15">September 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Kurt_Wolff_(aviator)" title="Kurt Wolff (aviator)">Kurt Wolff</a>, German World War I fighter ace (killed in action) (b. <a href="/wiki/1895" title="1895">1895</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_23" title="September 23">September 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Werner_Voss" title="Werner Voss">Werner Voss</a>, German World War I fighter ace (killed in action) (b. <a href="/wiki/1897" title="1897">1897</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_27" title="September 27">September 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Degas" title="Edgar Degas">Edgar Degas</a>, French painter (b. <a href="/wiki/1834" title="1834">1834</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_30" title="September 30">September 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Patricio_Montojo_y_Pasar%C3%B3n" title="Patricio Montojo y Pasarón">Patricio Montojo y Pasarón</a>, Spanish admiral (b. <a href="/wiki/1839" title="1839">1839</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span id="October–December"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="October.E2.80.93December">October–December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: October–December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
