<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_9" title="October 9">October 9</a> – Sultan <a href="/wiki/Hussein_Kamel_of_Egypt" title="Hussein Kamel of Egypt">Hussein Kamel of Egypt</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1853" title="1853">1853</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_11" title="October 11">October 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Duke_Philipp_of_Wurttemberg" class="mw-redirect" title="Duke Philipp of Wurttemberg">Duke Philipp of Wurttemberg</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1838" title="1838">1838</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_13" title="October 13">October 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Florence_La_Badie" title="Florence La Badie">Florence La Badie</a>, American actress (accident) (b. <a href="/wiki/1888" title="1888">1888</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_15" title="October 15">October 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/Mata_Hari" title="Mata Hari">Mata Hari</a>, Dutch dancer and spy (executed) (b. <a href="/wiki/1876" title="1876">1876</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_17" title="October 17">October 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Atherton" title="Bobby Atherton">Bobby Atherton</a>, Welsh footballer (b. <a href="/wiki/1876" title="1876">1876</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_22" title="October 22">October 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bob_Fitzsimmons" title="Bob Fitzsimmons">Bob Fitzsimmons</a>, British boxer, World Heavyweight Champion (b. <a href="/wiki/1863" title="1863">1863</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Eug%C3%A8ne_Grasset" title="Eugène Grasset">Eugène Grasset</a>, Swiss artist (b. <a href="/wiki/1845" title="1845">1845</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_27" title="October 27">October 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Rhys-Davids" title="Arthur Rhys-Davids">Arthur Rhys-Davids</a>, British fighter ace (killed in action) (b. <a href="/wiki/1897" title="1897">1897</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_28" title="October 28">October 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Prince_Christian_of_Schleswig-Holstein" title="Prince Christian of Schleswig-Holstein">Prince Christian of Schleswig-Holstein</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1831" title="1831">1831</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_30" title="October 30">October 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Heinrich_Gontermann" title="Heinrich Gontermann">Heinrich Gontermann</a>, German fighter ace (flying accident) (b. <a href="/wiki/1896" title="1896">1896</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_3" title="November 3">November 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/Frederick_Rodgers" title="Frederick Rodgers">Frederick Rodgers</a>, American admiral (b. <a href="/wiki/1842" title="1842">1842</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_8" title="November 8">November 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Colin_Blythe" title="Colin Blythe">Colin Blythe</a>, English cricketer (b. <a href="/wiki/1879" title="1879">1879</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_11" title="November 11">November 11</a> – Queen <a href="/wiki/Liliuokalani" title="Liliuokalani">Liliuokalani</a>, last monarch of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Hawaii" title="Kingdom of Hawaii">Kingdom of Hawaii</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1838" title="1838">1838</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_15" title="November 15">November 15</a> – <a href="/wiki/%C3%89mile_Durkheim" title="Émile Durkheim">Émile Durkheim</a>, French sociologist (b. <a href="/wiki/1858" title="1858">1858</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_17" title="November 17">November 17</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Neil_Primrose_(politician)" title="Neil Primrose (politician)">Neil Primrose</a>, British Liberal MP (killed in action) (b. <a href="/wiki/1882" title="1882">1882</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Auguste_Rodin" title="Auguste Rodin">Auguste Rodin</a>, French sculptor (b. <a href="/wiki/1840" title="1840">1840</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_8" title="December 8">December 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Mendele_Mocher_Sforim" title="Mendele Mocher Sforim">Mendele Mocher Sforim</a>, Russian Yiddish and Hebrew writer (b. <a href="/wiki/1836" title="1836">1836</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_10" title="December 10">December 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/Mackenzie_Bowell" title="Mackenzie Bowell">Mackenzie Bowell</a>, 5th <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister of Canada</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1823" title="1823">1823</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_12" title="December 12">December 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Taylor_Still" title="Andrew Taylor Still">Andrew Taylor Still</a>, American father of osteopathy (b. <a href="/wiki/1828" title="1828">1828</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Richard_Maybery" title="Richard Maybery">Richard Maybery</a>, British fighter ace (killed in action) (b. <a href="/wiki/1895" title="1895">1895</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_20" title="December 20">December 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Eric_Campbell_(actor)" title="Eric Campbell (actor)">Eric Campbell</a>, Scottish actor (accident) (b. <a href="/wiki/1879" title="1879">1879</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_22" title="December 22">December 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/Frances_Xavier_Cabrini" title="Frances Xavier Cabrini">Frances Xavier Cabrini</a>, first American canonized as a saint (b. <a href="/wiki/1850" title="1850">1850</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_24" title="December 24">December 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Goremykin" title="Ivan Goremykin">Ivan Goremykin</a>, Russian statesman, former Prime Minister (b. <a href="/wiki/1839" title="1839">1839</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_28" title="December 28">December 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Alfred_Edwin_McKay" title="Alfred Edwin McKay">Alfred Edwin McKay</a>, Canadian fighter ace (killed in action) (b. <a href="/wiki/1892" title="1892">1892</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nobel_Prizes">Nobel Prizes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1917&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Nobel Prizes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="floatright"><a href="/wiki/File:Nobel_medal.png" class="image"><img alt="Nobel medal.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/100px-Nobel_medal.png" width="100" height="100" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/150px-Nobel_medal.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/200px-Nobel_medal.png 2x" data-file-width="1013" data-file-height="1013" /></a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physics" title="Nobel Prize in Physics">Physics</a> – <a href="/wiki/Charles_Glover_Barkla" title="Charles Glover Barkla">Charles Glover Barkla</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Chemistry" title="Nobel Prize in Chemistry">Chemistry</a> – not awarded</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physiology_or_Medicine" title="Nobel Prize in Physiology or Medicine">Medicine</a> – not awarded</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Literature" title="Nobel Prize in Literature">Literature</a> – <a href="/wiki/Karl_Adolph_Gjellerup" title="Karl Adolph Gjellerup">Karl Adolph Gjellerup</a>, <a href="/wiki/Henrik_Pontoppidan" title="Henrik Pontoppidan">Henrik Pontoppidan</a></li>
